<Review>tl/dr: Find a different insurance company. Insurance companies who provided fast and good service to friends and family after the Carr Fire: Farmers, State Farm, and Progressive.

After the Carr fire I contacted Carly Pickern's office and submitted an insurance claim due to smoke and ash damages to my house due to the Carr Fire, which was declared a state of emergency. During the fire, my house and the homes of my neighbors were covered with black smoke, ash, high heat temperatures, and was inundated with harmful and poisonous particulates and literal burnt pieces of homes that were lost in my neighborhood and surrounding homes. Overall, ash, burnt home debris and thick smoke covered my home from early July to Mid-October 2018.

Carly Pickern's office basically insured my home through a third party, Pacific Specialty, so I was directed to speak with them about my claim.

After submitting the claim, I spent several months on the phone and over emails with Pacific Specialty Insurance trying to make my position on the claim that my house needs the appropriate attention by fire and smoke restoration cleaning company. My claim was evaluated, by Pacific Specialty, and they came to the conclusion that they would only clean the outside of my home and denied any cleaning of the interior of my home, specifically the carpet, floors, and walls. I have two children so I was concerned about the ash and poisonous material that entered my home and was covering my floors, walls, and possibly furniture. Two separate inspectors from Service Master came on two separate occasions, once at my request and once at the Pacific Specialty's request. They both stated by home should be cleaned top to bottom. Pacific Specialty disagreed and offered a payment in the amount of $2854.77 minus $1000.0 deductible to clean the exterior of the home.

After Pacific Specialty refused to clean the interior of my home, I contacted Carly Pickern's office and spoke to her. She said she agreed with my claim and apologized for issues I was having with Pacific Specialty. She said she would contact them and attempt to resolve the issue. She contacted me a few days later and let me know there was nothing she could do and that I would just have to fight the claim with Pacific Specialty.

So while the majority of my issue is with Pacific Specialty, this problem also with them also reflects on Allstate and Carly's office. It made me think, "Why am I paying her office if she is unable to assist with home insurance related issues? Why am I paying her office so she can insure me through another company?"

In addition to the above information, I spoke with friends and family who all had insurance related claims. Every single one of them informed me their insurance company's called them within a few days of the fire and evacuation to ask if they were ok and if they would like to file a claim. Carly's office never contacted me prior to my call to them. Further, they all received payouts extremely fast in order to resolve their ash, smoke, suit issues.

I was finally paid out this month (May 2019) after filing the original claim in July 2018. I had to go through the California Department of Insurance and deal with lawyers before they decided to provide an insurance payment. I received much less then what was needed, but I was tired of dealing with this issue and just wanted it resolved.</Review><date>1558482153853<//date>< user_id>

< Review>
Where to begin This place is failing on all levels. AVOID AT ALL COSTS!! HORRIBLE FOOD, HORRIBLE SERVICE, HORRIBLE OWNER !!! BEWARE YOU WILL GET SICK !!!!!
I took my family here for a meal yesterday and I would have been better off going to Jack in a Box for Steak.

We walked in and were seated our waitress couldn't have been more rude or brainless she didn't even introduce herself so I couldn't tell you her name. She was talking our order fighting about prices and didn't even know there own menu.

Ordered a Filet without bacon medium rare
got bacon wrapped over done filet
Sent it back
asked for the manger and was informed they have the owner there
she walks to the other waitress and says oh they just want to complain
owner comes out tells me I shouldn't complain before I get my food and brings to the table an
over done Filet
I send it back
everyone else at the Table is now eating
I get another steak brought out by the owner now raw different color than all the other filets that have been brought to my table and different size. There's no way in hell I got a filet the meat was rubbery salty and horrible. The baked potato was yellow and could tell that it was left over from the day before.
Not only did I have to pay full price but we were treated like trash.
*this didn't happen to me but the poor old woman and her son were there at the same time as we were she had her breathing machine the same brainless waitress took their order they went to the bathroom and when they had come back the stupid waitress had sat other people in their seats they were so upset and she couldn't hardly walk.

After we left  we all got horrible food poisoning puking diarrhea the whole nine yards. Called to speak with the owner and he hung up on us 3 yes 3 times and refuses to give us a refund for horrible service and making us sick.

So in conclusion if you would like to eat food you wouldn't even serve to a dog and be belittled this is the place to go. Also be ready to be sick and get falsely advertised pieces of meat. if you can call it that.

To the owner of Steer N Ale do everyone a favor and close the door you have no idea what a steakhouse is supposed to be plus you are rude and obviously not a good business man.<//Review>

< Text>
Well this is the first time that I've gone to Tacos Mexico. I found myself on the road headed home and wanted to eat. But I did not want to eat my regular burger or fast food. I just happened to be passing by Taco Mexico next to the entrance to the Highway 15 South so I decide to go there and get a couple tacos. I noticed that the tacos were a little small so I got a burrito to go along with it. The people that work there were friendly and courteous I received my taco my burrito and some green sauce and some napkins and my soda. All I can say the food tasted great to me I had no complaints at all. And I invite everyone in the area. I would invite everyone in the area to give it a try. Good things come in small packages and restaurants it appears. Enjoy
Oh the only reason that I gave a Taco Mexico 4 out of 5 Stars was that the whole time I was there I was a bit cold I think the air conditioner was on and it was still just know just a little bit cold for me otherwise I enjoy the whole time I was there. And the bathroom was clean.
